Testregel 2.1.1 (2.1.1 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

<span> with onclick has no tabindex - not keyboard focusable

<span class="close" onclick="closeLogin()"></span>
Add tabindex='0' to make element focusable, or use a button/link

2.4.3 Fokusrekkefølge (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.3 (2.4.3 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Positive tabindex (1) disrupts natural focus order

<a href="#secMain" tabindex="1">Gå til innhold</a>
Use tabindex='0' for focusable elements or '-1' for programmatic focus only
2.4.1 Hopp over blokker (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.1 (2.4.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Page has no skip link to bypass navigation

<body>
Add a skip link at the start of the page: <a href='#main'>Hopp til hovedinnhold</a>

Use native <a> semantics or change to appropriate element

CRITICAL

<span> with onclick has no tabindex - not keyboard focusable

2.4.3 Fokusrekkefølge (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.3 (2.4.3 - Nivå A)

Use tabindex='0' for focusable elements or '-1' for programmatic focus only

<body>

2.1.1 Tastatur (4 avvik)
Testregel 2.1.1 (2.1.1 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

<span> with onclick has no tabindex - not keyboard focusable

<span class="close" onclick="closeLogin()"></span>
Add tabindex='0' to make element focusable, or use a button/link
Testregel 2.1.1 (2.1.1 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

<span class="close" onclick="closeLogin()"></span>
Add tabindex='0' to make element focusable, or use a button/link

2.4.3 Fokusrekkefølge (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.3 (2.4.3 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Positive tabindex (1) disrupts natural focus order

<a href="#secMain" tabindex="1">Gå til innhold</a>
Use tabindex='0' for focusable elements or '-1' for programmatic focus only
2.4.1 Hopp over blokker (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.1 (2.4.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Page has no skip link to bypass navigation

<body>
Add a skip link at the start of the page: <a href='#main'>Hopp til hovedinnhold</a>
4.1.1 Parsing (1 avvik)
Testregel 4.1.1 (4.1.1 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Duplicate ID found: '175969' appears 2 times

id="175969"
Each ID must be unique on the page

Testregel 4.1.2 (4.1.2 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

<a> element has conflicting role='button'

2.4.3 Fokusrekkefølge (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.3 (2.4.3 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Positive tabindex (1) disrupts natural focus order

<a href="#secMain" tabindex="1">Gå til innhold</a>
Use tabindex='0' for focusable elements or '-1' for programmatic focus only
